./env/lib/python3.13/site-packages/pandas/plotting/_core.py:    is that it can also work with other third-party backends. This function
./env/lib/python3.13/site-packages/pandas/plotting/_core.py:    actually do the plotting. The backend is specified from a string, which
./env/lib/python3.13/site-packages/pandas/plotting/_core.py:    either comes from the keyword argument `backend`, or, if not specified, from
./env/lib/python3.13/site-packages/pandas/plotting/_core.py:    the option `pandas.options.plotting.backend`. All the rest of the code in
./env/lib/python3.13/site-packages/pandas/plotting/_core.py:    this file uses the backend specified there for the plotting.
./env/lib/python3.13/site-packages/pandas/plotting/_core.py:    The backend is imported lazily, as matplotlib is a soft dependency, and
